//Bayoen

// 攻撃する気をなくす

A spell that deeply moves a monster, preventing attack.

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B903, 0xB903)
#SETINDEXLIST(0x5)

//Lwark Void

// 魔物の守りを[br]
// 弱らせる呪文
A spell that reduces the defense of a monster.
[end]

#ENDSCRIPT()

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B91D, 0xB91D)
#SETINDEXLIST(0x6)

//Revia

// 受けたダメージを[br]
// 魔物にも与える呪文
A spell that reflects received damage back to the monster.
[end]

#ENDSCRIPT()

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B941, 0xB941)
#SETINDEXLIST(0x7)

//Sleep

// 魔物を　静かに[br]
// 眠らせる呪文
A spell that puts a monster to sleep.
[end]

#ENDSCRIPT()

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B95D, 0xB95D)
#SETINDEXLIST(0x8)

//Braindumbed

// 魔物の頭を弱らせて攻撃の手を
A spell that weakens a monster's brain,
[wait]

[clear_goto_line2]
// 緩めさせる呪文
reducing their offensive abilities.
[end]

#ENDSCRIPT()

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B98A, 0xB98A)
#SETINDEXLIST(0x9)

//Jugem

// 当たれば死ぬ　でも[br]
// なかなか当たらない
//A powerful spell that will defeat a monster.[br]
//However, it has a very low rate of success.
A powerful spell that will defeat a monster.
[wait]
[clear_goto_line2]
However, it has a very low rate of success.
[end]

#ENDSCRIPT()

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B9B0, 0xB9B0)
#SETINDEXLIST(0xA)

//Healing

// 元気になる呪文
A spell that heals your injuries.
[end]

#ENDSCRIPT()

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B9BF, 0xB9BF)
#SETINDEXLIST(0xB)

//Warp

// 上階に移動する呪文[br]
// 出来ない事もある
//A spell that moves you one floor above.[br]
//There are places where it will not work.
A spell that moves you one floor above.
[wait]
[clear_goto_line2]
There are places where it will not work.
[end]

#ENDSCRIPT()

//[TEXT]
#STARTSCRIPT(0x1B9E3, 0xB9E3)
